RESUMO 

O presente trabalho parte da problem√°tica de que h√° diverg√™ncias e confus√µes em torno dos 

conceitos de isometria e de simetria nos Par√¢metros Curriculares Nacionais ‚Äì PCNs, na Base 

Nacional Comum Curricular ‚Äì BNCC, em cole√ß√µes de livros did√°ticos e em livros destinados 

principalmente  a  professores  de  matem√°tica.  Considerando  essa  problem√°tica,  foi  realizada 

uma pesquisa meta-an√°lise para investigar a quest√£o: Qual a rela√ß√£o entre isometria e simetria 

de figuras planas? Para isso, uma amostra de onze obras foram analisadas. Sete delas, s√£o os 

livros mais citados em uma amostra de 74 disserta√ß√µes, teses ou artigos, que t√™m como assunto 

principal as isometrias e/ou simetrias. As outras quatro obras est√£o relacionadas ao contexto do 

Movimento da Matem√°tica Moderna - MMM, pois foi nesse movimento que as isometrias e 

simetrias foram inseridas no curr√≠culo da Educa√ß√£o B√°sica. A fundamenta√ß√£o te√≥rica se baseou 

na Teoria dos Registros de Representa√ß√µes Semi√≥ticas de Raymond Duval. Em especial, foram 

realizados  tratamentos  nos  registros  das  l√≠nguas  (l√≠ngua  natural  e  formal)  para  comparar 

defini√ß√µes e conceitos, e realizadas convers√µes entre representa√ß√µes nos registros alg√©brico e 

figural e vice-versa, para comparar e explicar conceitos e fazer demonstra√ß√µes. A investiga√ß√£o 

da rela√ß√£o entre isometria e simetria envolveu discuss√µes sobre a classifica√ß√£o das isometrias e 

simetrias, sobre a simetria e a figura sim√©trica, al√©m de uma retomada dos assuntos de fun√ß√µes 

e  estruturas  alg√©bricas,  principalmente  grupos  diedrais  e  c√≠clicos.  Os  resultados  das  obras 

analisadas  e  o  confronto  dos  dados  mostram  que  n√£o  h√°  diverg√™ncias  sobre  o  conceito  de 

isometria,  pois  todos  os  autores  concordam  direta  ou  indiretamente  que  isometria  √©  uma 

transforma√ß√£o  geom√©trica  que  preserva  dist√¢ncias.  Contudo,  o  mesmo  n√£o  ocorre  com  o 

conceito de simetria e as classifica√ß√µes das isometrias e simetrias, sendo que essas diverg√™ncias 

implicaram em uma confus√£o sobre a rela√ß√£o entre isometria e simetria. Desta forma, a simetria 

se apoia no conceito de invari√¢ncia, por este ser mais preciso formalmente, por estar intr√≠nseco 

ao estudo de estruturas alg√©bricas e pelo fato de que todas as outras interpreta√ß√µes sobre simetria 

que omitem ou ignoram o conceito de invari√¢ncia, acabam gerando confus√µes. 

Palavras-Chave: Transla√ß√£o; Rota√ß√£o; Reflex√£o; Transforma√ß√µes Geom√©tricas. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
ABSTRACT 

The actual assignment is based on the problem that there are divergences and confusions 

about the concepts of isometry and symmetry at Par√¢metros Curriculares Nacionais‚Äì PCNs at 

Base  Nacional  Comum  Curricular  ‚Äì  BNCC,  in  textbook  collections  and  in  books  intended 

mainly for mathematics teachers. Considering this problematic topic, it was conducted a meta-

analysis  research  to  investigate  the  issue:  What  is  the  relationship  between  isometry  and 

symmetry of flat shapes? So, a sample of eleven works were analyzed. Seven of them are the 

most cited books in a sample of 74 dissertations, theses, or articles, which they have as main 

subject the isometry and/or symmetries. The other four works are related to the context of the 

New  Mathematics  Movement,  because  it  was  in  this  movement  that  the  isometry  and 

symmetries were inserted in the curriculum of Basic Education. The theoretical foundation was 

based on Raymond Duval's Theory of Semiotic Representation of Records. In special, it was 

performed  treatments  in  the  language  records  (natural  and  formal  language)  to  compare 

definitions and concepts, and conversions were performed between representations in algebraic 

and figural records and vice versa, to compare and explain concepts and have demonstrations. 

The investigation of the relationship between isometry and symmetry involved discussions on 

the  classification  of  isometries  and  symmetries,  about  symmetry  and  symmetrical  figure,  in 

addition to a resumption of the subjects of algebraic functions and structures, mainly dihedral 

and cyclic groups. The results of the analyzed works and the comparison of the data show us 

that there are no divergences on the concept of isometry because all the authors agree directly 

or indirectly that isometry is a geometric transformation which preserves distances. However, 

the same does not occur with the concept of symmetry and the classifications of isometry and 

symmetries, so these divergences implied a confusion about the relationship between isometry 

and symmetry. Thus, the symmetry is based on the concept of invariance because it is more 

formally  accurate, because it is  intrinsic to  the study of algebraic structures and because  all 

other  interpretations  about  symmetry  that  omit  or  ignore  the  concept  of  invariance  end  up 

generating confusion.  

Keywords: Translation; Rotation; Reflection; Geometric Transformations

4.1 INTRODU√á√ÉO
